### [66] [Approximating optimal decoding of quantum LDPC codes with narrow frontiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20513)
*Anthony Leverrier,Rüdiger Urbanke*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了Frontier解码器，一种用于稀疏量子解码问题的剪枝动态规划解码器。它按顺序处理错误变量，合并具有相同残留综合征和逻辑标签的前缀，并通过仅保留狭窄的得分前沿来近似逻辑陪集后验质量。在代码容量设置中，该解码器在表面码和颜色码上达到了接近最优的阈值。在电路级噪声模型中，它以非常小的平均保留列表大小（gross code [[144,12,12]]在物理错误率0.001时小于100）实现了最先进的性能。当列表大小恒定时，解码器具有线性复杂度，暗示了低延迟实现的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子解码问题在稀疏情况下计算复杂度高，现有解码器难以同时实现高精度和低延迟。作者希望设计一种在保持接近最优解码阈值的同时，具有线性复杂度、适合低延迟实现的解码方案。

Method: Frontier解码器采用剪枝动态规划方法：按选定顺序处理错误变量，合并具有相同残留综合征和逻辑标签的前缀状态，并通过仅保留一个狭窄的得分前沿来近似逻辑陪集后验质量。未剪枝时，该递归即为具有指数复杂度的精确有序推理。

Result: 在代码容量设置下，表面码和颜色码的解码阈值接近最优；在电路级噪声模型下，gross code [[144,12,12]]在物理错误率0.001时平均保留列表大小不到100，达到最先进性能。当列表大小固定时，解码器复杂度为线性。

Conclusion: Frontier解码器在稀疏量子解码中实现了精度与效率的良好平衡，线性复杂度特性使其具备低延迟实现的潜力，适用于实际量子计算系统中的实时解码需求。

Abstract: We introduce the Frontier decoder, a pruned dynamic-programming decoder for sparse quantum decoding problems. Frontier processes error variables in a chosen order, merges prefixes with the same residual syndrome and logical label, and approximates logical-coset posterior masses by retaining only a narrow scored frontier. Without pruning, the recursion is exact ordered inference with exponential complexity.
  In the code-capacity setting, the decoder reaches thresholds close to optimal for the surface code and the color code. In the circuit-level noise model, it achieves state-of-the-art performance with a very small average retained list size: less than 100 for the gross code $[[144,12,12]]$ at a physical error rate of $0.001$. When the list size is constant, the decoder has linear complexity, suggesting the possibility of low-latency implementations.

### [67] [GPU-accelerated semidefinite programming for causal games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20519)
*Emanuel-Cristian Boghiu,Kyrylo Simonov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过GPU加速的半正定规划算法，研究Guess-Your-Neighbour's-Input游戏中局部维度从d=5扩展到d=8对获胜概率的影响，发现性能提升有限，暗示要么需要全新策略来逼近已知上界0.7592，要么上界本身不紧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究增大局部维度能否缩小当前最佳策略（d=5时约0.6218）与已知最强上界（0.7592）之间的差距，以理解量子因果关联的极限。

Method: 采用see-saw优化方案，每步建模为半正定规划；为提升可扩展性，开发了定制SCS求解器，将正半定锥投影这一主要计算开销卸载到GPU上，实现6倍加速，并测试了d=5至d=8的局部维度。

Result: 在d=8的局部维度下，未发现显著优于d=5的性能提升。

Conclusion: 当前结果暗示，要逼近已知上界0.7592，可能需要定性不同的策略，或者该上界本身并非紧界。

Abstract: The process matrix formalism describes quantum correlations in scenarios without a fixed causal order between local laboratories. Operational signatures of such correlations can be investigated through causal games. A paradigmatic example is the Guess-Your-Neighbour's-Input game, in which two parties attempt to guess each other's inputs. Correlations compatible with any definite, or probabilistically mixed, causal order cannot achieve a winning probability exceeding $1/2$. The best process-matrix strategy currently known attains a value of approximately $0.6218$ using local dimension $d=5$, while the strongest known dimension-independent upper bound is $0.7592$. In this work, we investigate whether increasing the local dimension beyond $d = 5$ can narrow this gap. To this end, we employ a see-saw optimization scheme in which each step is formulated as a semidefinite program. For scalability, we develop a custom implementation of the SCS solver in which the dominant computational cost, the projection onto the positive-semidefinite cone, is offloaded to a GPU, yielding a six-fold speedup. Using this implementation, we explore local dimensions up to $d = 8$, and we do not find significant improvements over the value at $d=5$. Our results suggest that either qualitatively different strategies are required to approach the known upper bound, or that the bound itself is not tight.

</details>


### [68] [Near-Optimal Learning of Local Lindbladians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20535)
*Itai Arad,Zhili Chen,Naixu Guo,Patrick Rebentrost,Zhan Yu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从黑盒动力学中学习局域Lindbladians的算法，通过有限时间信道探测、经典阴影估计和局域傅里叶反演来估算所有哈密顿量和耗散系数。算法在局域动力学强度界Λ和目标精度ε下，动力学演化使用次数为Õ(Λ²/ε²)，总演化时间为Õ(Λ/ε²)，且仅对数依赖于量子比特数。同时给出了匹配的下界，证明该算法在物理动力学访问和总演化时间上近乎最优，并指出海森堡极限在存在耗散时信息论上不可达。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子系统学习主要关注哈密顿量学习（纯酉演化），但真实开放量子系统同时包含哈密顿量和耗散过程。目前缺乏从黑盒动力学中高效学习完整Lindbladians（包括耗散系数）的算法，且不清楚耗散存在时学习的基本极限。

Method: 1) 对未知演化施加短时间探测；2) 利用经典阴影协议从随机乘积态输入和随机泡利测量中估计对应泡利转移矩阵；3) 通过稳定的局域傅里叶反演将估计值转换为Lindbladian系数。算法非自适应、无需辅助比特、无需预知Lindbladian支撑。

Result: 算法所需动力学演化次数为Õ(Λ²/ε²)，总演化时间为Õ(Λ/ε²)，仅对数依赖于系统规模；同时证明单量子比特退相位Lindbladian族需要Ω(Λ²/ε²)次信道使用和Ω(Λ/ε²)总演化时间，表明算法近乎最优，且哈密顿量学习中的海森堡极限在耗散估计中不可实现。

Conclusion: 该工作首次给出了从黑盒动力学中学习局域Lindbladians的高效算法及其信息论下界，建立了开放量子系统学习的理论极限，揭示了耗散过程对学习基本瓶颈的根本性影响。

Abstract: We study the problem of learning local Lindbladians from black-box access to the physical evolution, and the goal is to estimate all Hamiltonian and dissipative coefficients. We give an algorithm built directly from finite-time channel probes, which runs the unknown evolution for short times, estimates the corresponding Pauli transfer matrices from classical shadows, and converts these estimates into Lindbladian coefficients by stable local Fourier inversions. For fixed locality and bounded dissipative site degree, the uses of the dynamical evolution and total evolution time scale as $\widetilde{O}(Λ^2/\varepsilon^2)$ and $\widetilde{O}(Λ/\varepsilon^2)$ respectively, in the local dynamical strength bound $Λ$ and target accuracy $\varepsilon$, with only logarithmic dependence on the number of qubits. The algorithm is non-adaptive, uses no ancillas, and uses only random product states as inputs followed by random Pauli measurements. The method does not require knowing the support of the Lindbladian in advance. We complement the algorithm with matching lower bounds, showing that the learning algorithm is near-optimal both in physical dynamics accesses and in total evolution time. We construct a single-qubit dephasing Lindbladian family that already requires $Ω(Λ^2/\varepsilon^2)$ channel uses and $Ω(Λ/\varepsilon^2)$ total evolution time, even for adaptive algorithms with arbitrary ancillas and measurements. In particular, the lower bounds imply that the Heisenberg-limited scaling achievable for Hamiltonian learning is information-theoretically impossible once dissipative coefficients must be estimated.

</details>


### [69] [Benchmark of quantum algorithms for ground state preparation in the presence of noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20551)
*Daniel Molpeceres,Sirui Lu,J. Ignacio Cirac,Barbara Kraus*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在存在退极化噪声的二次费米子哈密顿量模型中，系统比较了冷却、绝热和优化算法用于基态制备的性能。研究发现算法表现依赖于量子相：绝热演化在平凡相中优势明显，而多频冷却算法在拓扑相中因能隙闭合而更具竞争力。QAOA在平凡相中与冷却算法相当，但在拓扑相中表现较差。冷却协议还展现出对参数缺陷的更强鲁棒性。该分析框架可推广用于基态制备算法的基准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有噪声的实际量子计算环境中，系统评估和比较不同基态制备算法的性能，特别是研究它们在不同量子相（平凡相与拓扑相）下的表现差异及鲁棒性。

Method: 采用可精确求解的二次费米子哈密顿量族（存在退极化噪声），通过解析推导相对能量随噪声率的标度关系，并结合数值模拟验证。比较了绝热演化、多频冷却算法（文献[1]）和量子近似优化算法QAOA（文献[2]）的性能。

Result: 算法性能依赖于量子相：平凡相中绝热演化最优；拓扑相中因能隙闭合导致绝热协议受限，多频冷却算法更具竞争力或更优；QAOA在平凡相与冷却算法相当，但在拓扑相中通常被超越。冷却协议对参数缺陷具有更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 建立了结合解析推导与数值验证的可推广基准测试框架，为噪声环境下基态制备算法的评估提供了系统性方法，并指出冷却算法在拓扑相和鲁棒性方面的实际优势。

Abstract: We compare the performance of representative cooling, adiabatic, and optimization algorithms for ground-state preparation in the presence of noise. Using an exactly solvable family of quadratic fermionic Hamiltonians subject to depolarizing noise, we derive the scaling of the achievable relative energy as a function of the noise rate and support these results with numerical simulations. The Hamiltonian exhibits two phases, separated by a quantum phase transition. As expected, the performance of the different algorithms depends on the phase: adiabatic evolution is favorable in the trivial phase, while a multi-frequency cooling algorithm, as proposed in [1], becomes competitive or superior in the topological phase, where gap-closing limits adiabatic protocols. We further present numerical results for the quantum approximate optimization algorithm [2], showing that it performs competitively with cooling in the trivial phase but is typically outperformed in the topological regime. Finally, we show that for this model the cooling protocol exhibits enhanced robustness to parameter imperfections, highlighting its potential advantage for realistic implementations of noisy quantum state preparation.
  The analytical approach developed here, in conjunction with numerical validation, establishes an extendable approach to benchmarking ground-state preparation algorithms.

</details>

### [70] [One-point functions for $C_2$-cofinite VOAs: pseudo-traces and trace spaces of projective modules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19622)
*Max-Niklas Steffen*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文研究非有理 $C_2$-共有限顶点算子代数 $V$ 上环面单点函数空间，通过将其与 $V$ 表示范畴中投射对象子范畴的迹对象联系起来，并利用 Gainutdinov-Runkel 猜想，建立了迹空间对偶与投射生成子自同态代数 $E$ 上对称函数之间的联系，在分离共形权模 $\mathbb{Z}$ 条件下证明了单射性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非有理 $C_2$-共有限顶点算子代数上环面单点函数空间的结构，建立其与表示范畴中投射对象迹空间的对偶关系，并从表示论角度补充证明 Gainutdinov-Runkel 猜想。

Method: 将环面单点函数空间与投射对象的迹对象关联，利用 Arike-Nagatomo 伪迹方法，结合 Huang 的投射覆盖技术，构造 Gainutdinov-Runkel 映射并分别证明满射性和（在附加条件下）单射性。

Result: 证明了 Gainutdinov-Runkel 映射从 $E$ 上对称函数到单点函数空间的满射性；在共形权模 $\mathbb{Z}$ 分离条件下进一步证明了单射性。

Conclusion: 为非有理顶点算子代数上的环面单点函数提供了基于表示论的刻画，补充了 Gui 和 Zhang 用不同方法建立的 Gainutdinov-Runkel 猜想的结果。

Abstract: We study the space of one-point functions on the torus for a possibly nonrational $C_2$-cofinite vertex operator algebra $V$ by relating it to a trace object of the subcategory of projective objects in the representation category of $V$. We identify the dual of the trace space with symmetric functions on the endomorphism algebra $E$ of a projective generator. Motivated by the Gainutdinov-Runkel conjecture, recently established using different methods by Gui and Zhang, we present a complementary representation-theoretic approach based on Arike-Nagatomo pseudo-traces. In this framework, we prove surjectivity of the Gainutdinov-Runkel map from symmetric functions on $E$ to one-point functions. Under the additional assumption of separated conformal weights modulo $\mathbb{Z}$, we also prove injectivity, using projective-cover techniques inspired by Huang.

Result: 成功实现了扭曲量子环代数，包括Drinfeld新展示中的扭曲量子仿射代数。

Conclusion: 加权投影线的半导出Ringel-Hall代数可以用于实现更一般的扭曲量子环代数，推广了先前仅适用于单型（未扭曲）情形的工作。

Abstract: Twisted quantum loop algebras are a generalization of twisted quantum affine algebras in Drinfeld new presentation. ### [72] [Geometric realization of affine bases: the Kronecker quiver case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19708)
*Yumeng Wu,Jie Xiao*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文从几何角度研究了Kronecker箭图量子包络代数负部的PBW基与典范基之间的转移矩阵。基于Lusztig的典范基几何构造，作者通过表示簇分层上的旗层复形实现了PBW基元素，并利用相交上同调复形在子分层上的限制给出了转移系数的几何解释，证明了转移矩阵为上三角且对角元为1，在Kronecker箭图情形下恢复了转移矩阵的三角性并得到了系数多项式的正性。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the transition matrix between the PBW basis and the canonical basis for the negative part of the quantized enveloping algebra of the Kronecker quiver from a geometric viewpoint. Building on Lusztig's geometric construction of the canonical basis, we construct sheaf-complex realizations of PBW basis elements by means of flag sheaf complexes over the strata $X(α,m)$ of representation varieties. Our first goal is to give a geometric description of the simple constituents appearing in the restrictions of these flag sheaf complexes to the strata $X(α,m)$. This allows us to compare the PBW-type sheaf complexes with the simple perverse sheaves $IC(X(α),L_χ)$ arising in Lusztig's construction. Using this description together with a purity result for the relevant $\mathbb{F}_q$-structures, we obtain another proof that the elements defined by Lusztig's perverse sheaves indeed form a basis of the composition algebra.Our second goal is to make the transition coefficients between the PBW basis and the canonical basis geometrically explicit. More precisely, we show that these coefficients are governed by the multiplicities of local systems in the restrictions of intersection cohomology complexes to smaller strata. As a consequence, the transition matrix from the canonical basis to the PBW basis is upper triangular with diagonal entries equal to $1$, and its coefficients admit a direct geometric interpretation. In particular, in the Kronecker quiver case we recover the triangularity of the transition matrix and obtain positivity properties of the corresponding coefficient polynomials.

For affine Lie algebras of type $C_n^{(1)}$, such combinatorially parametrized relations among relations were constructed in earlier work for level $2$ standard modules \cite{PS3}, and for $C_2^{(1)}$-standard modules at higher levels \cite{S}. This article presents two further examples in which the same counting method can be carried out. The first treats $C_n^{(1)}$-standard modules at the fixed level $k=5$, with $n$ arbitrary. ### [74] [Cohomology of $\mathbf{GL}_d(\mathbb{F})$ in non-defining characteristic via the quantum schur algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20211)
*Theo Deturck*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文利用量子Schur代数计算一般线性群 $\mathbf{GL}_d(\mathbb{F})$ 在特定特征域 $\mathbb{k}$ 上的Ext群，突破了此前仅能计算度 $\leq \ell-1$ 上同调群的限制，对许多模可计算至更高次数（如 $3(\ell-1)$），并得到了量子Schur代数模间Ext群的新结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Let $G = \mathbf{GL}_d(\mathbb{F})$ be the general linear group over a field of cardinal $q$, and let $\mathbb{k}$ be a field of positive characteristic which does not divide $q(q-1)$. Building on the works of Cline, Parshall, and Scott, we show how to compute Ext-groups between $\mathbb{k}G$-modules using the quantum Schur algebra. The main novelty is our ability to compute these Ext-groups in higher degree than what was done before. More precisely, let $\ell$ be the order of $q$ in $\mathbb{k}$. In previous work, this method enabled the computation of the cohomology groups $H^*(\mathbf{GL}_d,M)$ in degree $*\leq \ell-1$. We show that for a lot of modules $M$, we can compute these cohomology groups in higher degree, with an example where we can compute until degree $3(\ell-1)$. The (meta-)stability of the Higgs vacuum may be pointing to some new critical phenomena at very high energy scales, with the Higgs connecting physics at LHC laboratory energies to that in the deep ultraviolet. In the emergence scenario, the dark energy scale comes out similar to the size of light Majorana neutrino masses. These two quantities appear at the same order in a low energy expansion in inverse powers of the scale of emergence, about $10^{16}$ GeV. Dark matter candidates include axions and phonon like excitations of degrees of freedom above the scale of emergence. Possible tests of these ideas involve neutrinos as well as gravitational-waves-related signals from the early Universe, which are sensitive to physics at very high energy scales.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: LeWRON采用智能体框架，包含审计工具箱构建模块和Explorer探索模块；中间分析结果由审计代理检查并存储为结构化工件；支持复现模式（从文献推断约定并复现结果）和发现模式（为新模型提供结构化检查点引导）；提供命令行界面和公开Python API。

Abstract: The electroweak phase transition (EWPT) is a central topic in particle physics and cosmology, connecting collider phenomenology, baryogenesis, and gravitational-wave observatories. Its analysis requires a technically demanding, convention-sensitive, and model-dependent pipeline, from constructing the finite-temperature effective potential to tracking thermal histories, computing bubble nucleation rates, and predicting gravitational-wave spectra. We present LeWRON (Learning ElectroWeak phase tRansitiON), an agentic framework that orchestrates this pipeline starting from an input Lagrangian. LeWRON combines audited toolbox construction with an Explorer module that uses the generated model-specific code for further analysis, including scans and plots. Intermediate analytic outputs are checked by auditor agents and stored as structured artifacts, enabling reproducible human inspection and downstream use through both a command-line interface and a public Python API. The framework supports a reproduction mode, which infers conventions from the literature and reproduces published results, and a discovery mode, which guides users through structured checkpoints for new models. We demonstrate LeWRON across representative beyond-the-Standard-Model scenarios and release the code on GitHub.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 提出的方法提供了系统性地计算无质量粒子理论中部分波幺正性边界的实用方案，克服了标准微扰论中前向散射奇异性带来的阻碍。

Abstract: Theories with massless particles contain $t$-channel (forward scattering) singularities that cause standard fixed order expressions for partial-wave amplitudes to be ill-defined. This presents an obstruction to systematically improvable partial-wave unitarity bounds. In this work, we study the construction of partial-wave amplitudes in a modified perturbation theory that incorporates long-range interactions focusing on the role of off-shell Coulomb modes. We find that there exists a universal description of the forward scattering region that renders the amplitudes renormalization scale independent. The resulting partial-wave amplitudes become well defined single-scale objects without spurious dependence on the infrared regulator, and we present a practical method for their computation order-by-order in perturbation theory.

For the QCD axion saturating the observed dark matter abundance, the nonlinear spectrum at equality exhibits two characteristic regions: one associated with the gravitational enhancement already present in moduli-driven cosmologies, and another produced by the temperature dependence of the axion mass. We estimate the resulting minicluster masses and discuss the possible formation of axion miniclusters and axion-star substructure.

*Kenji Nishiwaki,Kin-ya Oda,Juntaro Wada*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了真空中味振荡现象，通过鞍点法推导了短传播时间下的味改变振幅扩展表达式，发现振荡仅在传播时间超过由外部波包能量不确定度和传播粒子衰变宽度设定的阈值时发生。短传播时，中间粒子表现为纯虚态，无法在宏观距离上传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Jacob-Sachs（或Grimus-Stockinger）定理仅描述长传播时间（或距离）下简并中间态的振荡行为，缺乏对短传播时间情形下味振荡行为的完整理解。

Method: 采用波包量子场论框架，利用鞍点法显式评估相关积分，推导出适用于短传播时间的味改变振幅扩展表达式。

Result: 振荡仅在传播时间超过由外部波包能量不确定度和传播粒子衰变宽度设定的阈值时发生；短传播时中间粒子表现为纯虚态，无法宏观传播；Jacob-Sachs定理在短传播时间下仍具有比预期更高的精度。

Conclusion: 该形式不仅适用于中微子，也适用于其他传播粒子；未来能量分辨率的提升可能使该阈值变得可观测。

Abstract: We revisit flavor oscillations in vacuum in terms of the propagation time of intermediate states. In the limit of a long propagation time (or distance), degenerate intermediate states exhibit oscillatory behavior, as described by the Jacob--Sachs (or Grimus--Stockinger) theorem within wave-packet quantum field theory. By explicitly evaluating the relevant integrals using the saddle-point method, we derive an extended expression for the flavor-changing amplitude that remains valid even for shorter propagation times. We show that oscillations occur only when the propagation time exceeds a threshold set by the energy uncertainty of the external wave packets and by the decay width of the propagating particle. For shorter propagation, the intermediate particle behaves as a purely virtual state, in the sense that it cannot propagate over a macroscopic distance. Although a direct experimental test of the transition from virtual to real propagation is challenging, since it typically occurs at microscopic scales, our result implies that the Jacob--Sachs theorem holds to higher accuracy than previously expected, even at short propagation times. Our formalism applies not only to neutrinos but also to other propagating particles, and future improvements in energy resolution may make this threshold observable.

</details>


### [82] [Freeze-in at all couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19564)
*Andreas Goudelis,Andre Lessa,Lucas Magno Dantas Ramos,Thomas Reggio*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了带电母粒子“冻结”暗物质模型，重点关注宇宙再加热温度接近或低于理论质量标度的情形。在此构型中，暗物质产生受到玻尔兹曼抑制，允许暗物质与标准模型热浴之间存在更强耦合，同时仍能复现观测到的 relic 丰度。研究强调了再加热温度、中介子与暗物质质量及耦合强度之间非平凡的相互作用，并表明追踪暗物质和中介子两者的数密度演化对获得可靠预言至关重要。最后，更新了LHC搜索和轻子味破坏衰变的约束，展示了这些搜索在探测宇宙学可行参数空间中的互补性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有冻结暗物质模型通常假设再加热温度远高于暗物质质量标度，但对于再加热温度接近或低于质量标度的情形缺乏系统分析。在此低再热温度区域，暗物质产生受到玻尔兹曼抑制，允许更强的耦合强度，从而产生与高再热温度情形截然不同的现象学特征。本文旨在系统研究该未被充分探索的参数区域，揭示再加热温度、质量标度与耦合强度之间的复杂关联。

Method: 采用带电母粒子冻结暗物质模型，通过求解玻尔兹曼方程追踪暗物质和中介子两者的数密度演化，分析再加热温度接近或低于理论质量标度时暗物质的产生机制。方法强调：(1) 同时追踪暗物质和中介子的非平衡演化；(2) 考虑中介子因快速衰变而无法达到热平衡的异常行为；(3) 结合宇宙学约束和粒子物理实验约束进行参数空间扫描。

Result: (1) 低再加热温度下，玻尔兹曼抑制允许更强的耦合强度仍能复现观测暗物质丰度；(2) 发现了中介子因快速衰变而无法达到热平衡的非预期行为；(3) 更新了来自LHC搜索和轻子味破坏衰变（如μ→eγ）的实验约束，揭示了这些不同实验渠道在探测宇宙学允许参数空间方面的互补性。

Conclusion: 低再加热温度场景为冻结暗物质模型打开了更强的耦合区域，但这些区域受到LHC和轻子味破坏实验的严格约束。追踪多粒子数密度的联合演化是必要的，仅关注暗物质自身演化可能导致错误结论。不同实验搜索渠道的互补性对于全面探测该模型的可行参数空间至关重要。

Abstract: We perform a comprehensive analysis of a charged parent freeze-in dark matter model, focusing on scenarios where the Universe reheats to a temperature comparable to or lower than the mass scales of the theory. In such configurations, dark matter production is Boltzmann-suppressed, allowing for stronger couplings between dark matter and the Standard Model thermal bath while still reproducing the observed relic abundance. We emphasize the non-trivial interplay between the reheating temperature, the mediator and dark matter masses and the coupling strength. We show that tracking the number density evolution of both dark matter and the mediator is essential to obtain reliable predictions, including unexpected behaviors such as the mediator non-equilibration due to fast decays. Lastly, we explore the phenomenological implications of this scenario, updating constraints from LHC searches and lepton flavour-violating decays and highlighting the complementarity of these searches in probing the cosmologically viable parameter space.

</details>


### [83] [Sensitivity of the photon-induced processes to the proton radius](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19604)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用偶极子形状因子模型，比较常规 Λ²=0.71 GeV² 与 PDG 推荐的两个质子半径值（0.8751 fm 和 0.84087 fm）对应的测试场景；基于当前 ATLAS 和 CMS 实验数据进行拟合分析，提取有效质子半径。

Result: 拟合得到 Λ²=0.465±0.056 GeV²，对应的有效质子半径 r_p=1.002±0.038 fm；双轻子产生过程对质子半径尺度的灵敏度在大不变质量和前向/后向快度区域最为显著。

Conclusion: 该过程对质子半径具有非平凡的灵敏度，但当前结果尚不足以成为质子半径之谜的最终解决方案，需要更精确的实验数据和更完善的理论模型。

Abstract: We study the exclusive production of dileptons in proton--proton collisions as a probe of the proton radius. Using a dipole form factor model, we compare the conventional choice of $Λ^2=0.71$~GeV$^2$ with PDG test scenarios corresponding to $r_p=0.8751$~fm and $r_p=0.84087$~fm. The sensitivity is greatest at large dilepton invariant masses and forward/backward rapidity. Fitting to the current ATLAS and CMS data within the adopted model gives $Λ^2 = 0.465 \pm 0.056~\mathrm{GeV}^2$, corresponding to an effective radius $r_p = 1.002 \pm 0.038~\mathrm{fm}$, which indicates non-trivial sensitivity on the proton radius scale, but is not yet a definitive solution to the proton radius puzzle.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于超对称U(1)_{B-L}扩展标准模型，采用非最小Kähler势的平滑混合暴胀机制，引入三个标量场（暴胀子σ、辅助场ζ、中介单态η），通过Z_2对称性稳定惰性标量暗物质，暗物质通过再加热动力学非热产生。

Result: 观测到的暗物质遗迹丰度对暴胀参数施加强约束，将标量谱指数严格限制在n_s ≃ 0.972-0.974；暴胀-暗物质耦合对背景演化影响可忽略，但会显著改变张标比和原初引力波谱。

Conclusion: 暗物质产生与暴胀参数之间存在直接且可观测的关联，为在暴胀框架中检验暗物质模型提供了实验可验证的预言。

Abstract: We propose a unified framework that connects inflationary dynamics with dark matter production within a supersymmetric $U(1)_{B-L}$ extension of the Standard Model. The setup is based on smooth hybrid inflation embedded in supergravity, with a non-minimal Kahler potential ensuring control of higher-order corrections. The model involves three scalar fields: the inflaton $σ$, an auxiliary field $ζ$ responsible for ending inflation, and a singlet mediator $η$ that links the inflationary and dark sectors. Dark matter is realized as an inert scalar stabilized by a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry and produced non-thermally via reheating dynamics. We show that reproducing the observed dark matter relic abundance imposes strong constraints on the inflationary sector, significantly reducing the allowed parameter space. As a result, the scalar spectral index is tightly constrained to $n_s \simeq 0.972 - 0.974$, consistent with current observational bounds. While the inflaton-dark matter coupling has a negligible effect on the background evolution, it induces observable modifications in the tensor-to-scalar ratio and the spectrum of primordial gravitational waves. This establishes a direct link between dark matter physics and inflationary observables.

### [85] [Charged Lepton Flavor Violation at Neutrino Telescopes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19723)

Result: 给出了IceCube对相关EFT能标的灵敏度，以及在Z'质量-耦合平面上的灵敏度区间。结果表明，中微子望远镜的灵敏度可以与低能CLFV实验以及当前和未来对撞机实验的结果相比较，并可作为互补的探测手段。

Conclusion: 中微子望远镜能够为带电轻子味破坏搜索提供强有力的互补探测途径，特别是针对缪子到陶子转换过程，有望超越传统低能实验和对撞机实验在部分参数空间的灵敏度，体现出在天体粒子物理实验中探索新物理的潜力。

Abstract: Any observation of charged lepton flavor violation (CLFV) would be a clear signal of beyond-the-Standard-Model physics. Here, we propose a novel CLFV search using neutrino telescopes with their large cosmic-ray muon samples. Specifically, we use a recent IceCube cosmic-ray muon dataset and propose a new search for muon-to-tau conversion inside the IceCube detector. We illustrate our idea with CLFV interactions described by model-independent Effective Field Theory (EFT) operators and present the IceCube sensitivity on the relevant EFT scale. We also consider a specific realization of the EFT operator in terms of an axial-vector $Z'$ interaction and show sensitivities in the $Z'$ mass-coupling plane. We compare our sensitivities with those from low-energy CLFV searches, as well as from current and future collider experiments. We also show projections from next-generation neutrino telescopes, such as IceCube-Gen2 and HUNT, and demonstrate how neutrino telescopes can provide a powerful complementary probe of CLFV.

### [86] [Constraining ADD black holes at the LHC with $\sqrt{s} = 14$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19839)
*Ashfaque Ahmad,Sudhir Kumar Gupta,Abbas Ali*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在ADD模型框架下，利用LHC在质心能量14 TeV、积分光度349.4 fb⁻¹的数据，通过考虑黑洞形成过程中质量损失参数ζ，对微观黑洞质量M_B给出了约束。研究表明，当ζ=0且额外维数D=3时，M_B≤11.83 TeV的黑洞被排除（约化普朗克尺度Λ_D≈1 TeV）；Λ_D=9 TeV时对应限值为10.33 TeV。随着损失增加（ζ=0.35），M_B降至7.65(6.82) TeV（Λ_D=1(9) TeV）。当D增加到7时，上述限值在95%置信水平下分别变为12.03(10.88) TeV和7.80(7.03) TeV。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索额外维模型中微观黑洞在LHC上的可观测性，并量化黑洞形成过程中的质量损失效应对排除极限的影响。

Method: 基于ADD模型，利用LHC在√s=14 TeV、积分光度349.4 fb⁻¹的数据，引入参数ζ描述黑洞形成过程中的质量损失，对M_B施加约束，并分析不同额外维数D和约化普朗克尺度Λ_D下的排除极限。

Result: ζ=0时，D=3下M_B≤11.83 TeV被排除（Λ_D=1 TeV），Λ_D=9 TeV时对应10.33 TeV；ζ=0.35时，M_B降至7.65(6.82) TeV（Λ_D=1(9) TeV）。D=7时，ζ=0(0.35)对应95% C.L.限值为12.03(7.80) TeV（Λ_D=1 TeV）和10.88(7.03) TeV（Λ_D=9 TeV）。

Abstract: We explore microscopic black holes at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) in the context of the ADD model for the centre-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s} = 14~\mathrm{TeV}$ at an integrated luminosity of $349.4~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ and provide constraints on the black hole mass, $M_{\mathrm{B}}$ by taking into account the effects of loss during the formation process of black holes through the parameter $ζ$. Our analysis reveals that for $ζ= 0$, black holes with $M_{\mathrm{B}} \leq 11.83~\mathrm{TeV}$ are disfavored in the case of three extra dimensions ($\mathcal{D}$), for the reduced Planck scale ($Λ_{\mathcal{D}}$) of about a TeV. These limits change to $12.03 ~(10.88)~\mathrm{TeV}$ and $7.80~ (7.03)~\mathrm{TeV}$ respectively for $ζ= 0~(0.35)$ for $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 1 (9)~\mathrm{TeV}$ at 95\% C.L. in case $\mathcal{D}$ is raised to seven.

Abstract: We assess the tension between theoretical predictions and the values quoted by the Particle Data Group (PDG) for the partial decay width and branching fraction associated with the radiative charmonium decay $J/ψ\toγη_c$. We propose a theoretically grounded photon line shape for the radiative decay spectrum and a prescription for the extraction of (product) branching fractions involving the magnetic dipole (M1) transition $J/ψ\toγη_c$. This approach obviates the need to modify the photon energy spectrum line shape using empirical damping functions, as done in the most recent experimental extractions of $\mathcal{B}(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ from the photon line shape, thereby eliminating an inherent ambiguity in the determination of the derived observables.

### [88] [New Avenues of Heavy Neutral Lepton at Muon Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19906)
*Fa-Xin Yang,Feng-Lan Shao,Zhi-Long Han,Honglei Li*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统矢量玻色子融合过程（$WW/ZZ\to H\to NN$）受希格斯玻色子间小混合角 $\alpha$ 的抑制，信号强度受限。作者希望探索不依赖小混合角的新产生机制，以更有效地探测重中性轻子的内在特征。

Method: 在 $U(1)$ 规范扩展的跷跷板模型框架下，考虑多TeV缪子对撞机，研究通过新规范玻色子 $Z'$ 和重希格斯 $H$ 的矢量玻色子融合过程产生重中性轻子 $N$。分析了两种过程：有重希格斯参与的 $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ 和无重希格斯的 $Z'Z'\to NN$。信号末态为 $μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- NN$，随后 $N\to μ^\pm jj$，其中 $W$ 玻色子衰变的两个喷注合并为一个fat-jet $J$。

Result: 新过程 $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ 不受希格斯玻色子间小混合角 $\alpha$ 的抑制；无重希格斯的 $Z'Z'\to NN$ 过程在 $m_H > \sqrt{s}$ 时仍然有效。这两种新途径为探测重中性轻子提供了替代方案。

Conclusion: 在多TeV缪子对撞机上，通过新矢量玻色子融合产生重中性轻子的机制，克服了传统矢量玻色子融合过程中小混合角抑制的问题，提供了一种更有效的探测重中性轻子内在特征的方法。

Abstract: With initial state radiation, the multi-TeV muon collider can be regarded as an electroweak boson collider. The dominant production mode of the certain process becomes the vector boson fusion channel, because the corresponding cross section typically increases logarithmically at high energies. This also holds true for new physics beyond the standard model. Within the $U(1)$ gauged extension of seesaw models, the heavy neutral lepton has additional interactions with the new gauge boson $Z'$ and heavy Higgs $H$. In this paper, we investigate the production of heavy neutral lepton $N$ via the new vector boson fusion processes $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ with and $Z'Z'\to NN$ without heavy Higgs at the multi-TeV muon collider. Different from the canonical vector boson fusion processes $WW/ZZ\to H\to NN$, the new process $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ is not suppressed by the small mixing angle $α$ between the Higgs bosons. Meanwhile, the pair production process $Z'Z'\to NN$ is also viable even for heavy Higgs $m_H> \sqrt{s}$. Therefore, these new avenues provide alternative pathways to probe the intrinsic feature of the heavy neutral lepton. We then perform a detailed analysis of the lepton number violation signals via the new vector boson fusion with heavy Higgs $μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- H \to μ^+μ^- NN$ and without heavy Higgs $μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- NN$, followed by $N\to μ^\pm jj$, where the two jets from $W$ boson decay are treated as one fat-jet $J$.

</details>


### [89] [$Ξ_{cc}^{++}-Ξ_{cc}^{+}$ Transitions as a Two-Charm-Selective Portal to Ultra-Low-$Q$ Charged Currents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19991)
*Yong Du*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用LHCb观测到的$Ξ_{cc}^{+}$，研究了$Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$超低$Q$值跃迁作为带电电流新物理的零测试验。分析表明，对于MeV尺度反冲动量，该过程对有效重子能级耦合的灵敏度可达$10^{-6}-10^{-7}$量级。对于通用轻带电标量$φ^+$，现有电弱精密和β衰变约束已强于LHCb预期灵敏度，形成"无结果"结论。但作者找到了一个双粲选择性带电电流门户，其领先算符在双粲重子中非零，而在核子、原子核和单粲介子中领头阶为零，使$Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$跃迁成为该门户相互作用的领先直接探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHCb观测到$Ξ_{cc}^{+}$后，$Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$这一超低$Q$值跃迁为检验带电电流新物理提供了独特的实验窗口，作者希望利用该过程寻找超出标准模型的新物理信号。

Method: 采用二体和三体衰变分析，计算有效重子能级耦合的灵敏度；对比现有电弱精密测量和β衰变约束与LHCb投影灵敏度；识别并构造双粲选择性带电电流门户的有效算符。

Conclusion: $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$跃迁是检验带电电流新物理的有效零测试验，尤其适用于双粲选择性新物理门户，在此类模型中可提供领先的直接探测灵敏度。

Abstract: The recent LHCb observation of $Ξ_{cc}^{+}$ opens the ultra-low-$Q$ transition $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$ as an experimentally motivated null test of charged-current new physics. Our two- and three-body analyses show sensitivity to effective baryon-level couplings of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6}-10^{-7})$ for MeV-scale recoil momenta. We establish a practical no-go result for a universal light charged scalar $φ^+$: with a first-generation $φ^+\bar u d$ coupling, existing electroweak-precision and beta-decay constraints are parametrically stronger than the projected LHCb sensitivity. We then identify a two-charm-selective charged-current portal whose leading operator has a nonzero matrix element in doubly charmed baryons but vanishes at leading order in pions, nucleons, nuclei, and singly charmed mesons. In this class of models, $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$ transitions can provide the leading direct probe of the portal interaction.

In this work, we present a calculation of the NLO QCD and electroweak corrections to the process $\text{p}\text{p} \to \ell^+ ν_\ell + 4\text{j}$ in two different fiducial regions relevant for vector-boson scattering. In a fully off-shell calculation, we provide results for the leading electroweak contribution of $\mathcal{O}\left(α^6\right)$ and the corresponding corrections of $\mathcal{O}\left(α^7\right)$ and $\mathcal{O}\left(α_\text{s} α^6\right)$ for fiducial cross sections and a selection of differential distributions.

### [91] [Two Flavon Froggatt-Nielsen Models with Genetic Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20000)
*Miguel Crispim Romão,Stephen F. King*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次利用人工智能（NSGA-III遗传算法）系统扫描了两味标量场的Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) 风味模型。通过将CP破缺自然引入两味标量场框架，解决了单味标量场模型无法产生CP破缺的问题。该方法同时拟合18个FN电荷、45个Wilson系数及标量场参数，无需额外训练，比先前强化学习方法快数个数量级，发现了超过10万个唯象可行的唯一样本，并揭示了中微子质量顺序与无中微子双贝塔衰变有效质量$m_{ee}$之间的定性关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准单味标量场FN模型无法自然产生CP破缺；两味标量场框架的参数空间是混合离散-连续的高维空间，传统扫描方法无法有效探索。需要一种高效且系统的方法来扫描这一扩大的模型空间，并找到同时满足夸克和轻子 sector 所有实验约束的唯象可行模型。

Method: 将寻找唯象可行模型构造为多目标优化问题，每项实验约束作为独立目标；采用NSGA-III（非支配排序遗传算法III）同时优化18个FN电荷（离散）、45个Wilson系数（连续）及标量场参数。两味标量场分别独立耦合上型和下型费米子扇区，其真空期望值之间的相对相位自然提供CP破缺源。无需独立训练阶段。

Result: 发现超过10万个唯象可行的唯一样本，重复率极低，表明两味标量场FN模型的有效参数空间尚未被穷尽。同时实现了中微子质量的正序（NO）和反序（IO），标量场真空期望值之间的相对层级对无中微子双贝塔衰变有效质量$m_{ee}$产生定性不同的预言。发现了最大味子指数仅为3的最小FN实现，以及无需连续参数优化即可将带电费米子质量拟合到6%以内的模型。

Conclusion: 两味标量场FN模型是解释费米子质量层级和混合、以及CP破缺的丰富且尚未被完全探索的理论框架。人工智能驱动的多目标优化方法可高效探索此类高维混合参数空间，为未来味物理研究提供了强大的计算工具。

Abstract: We present the first systematic and comprehensive scan of two-flavon Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) models, employing artificial intelligence techniques to explore the high-dimensional, mixed discrete-continuous parameter space. Extending the standard single-flavon FN framework to a two-flavon setup in which separate flavon fields couple independently to the up- and down-type sectors, we demonstrate that the relative phase between their vacuum expectation values (vevs) provides a natural and generic source of CP violation absent in single-flavon models. To explore this enlarged model space, we cast the search for phenomenologically viable models as a multi-objective optimisation problem, formulating each experimental constraint as a separate objective, and employ the Non-dominated Sorting Genetic Algorithm III to simultaneously fit all 18 FN charges, 45 Wilson coefficients, and flavon parameters to both the quark and lepton sectors. Our approach requires no separate training phase and identifies phenomenologically viable models orders of magnitude faster than prior reinforcement learning methods. Imposing experimental constraints on CKM and PMNS mixing angles and CP phases, charged fermion masses, and neutrino squared-mass differences, we discover over $100\,000$ unique viable models with a remarkably low duplication rate, indicating that the space of valid two-flavon FN realisations has not been exhausted. Both Normal and Inverted neutrino mass squared orderings are realised, with the relative hierarchy between the flavon vevs producing qualitatively distinct predictions for the effective neutrinoless double beta decay mass $m_{ee}$. We further demonstrate the existence of minimal FN realisations with maximal flavon exponent as small as three, and of models reproducing charged fermion masses to within $6\%$ without any dedicated continuous parameter optimisation.

In such scenarios, vector-like Quarks (VLQs) can exhibit non-standard decay modes involving additional Higgs states, giving rise to distinctive collider signatures that remain largely unexplored by existing experimental searches. We investigate the prospects of probing this possibility at the high-luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC) through the decay of vector-like top partner ($T$) to charged Higgs ($H^{\pm}$) followed by the decay, $H^\pm\toτν$, producing a final state containing two tau leptons, two $b$-jets, and missing transverse energy. A model-independent collider analysis is performed using global kinematic observables constructed from visible objects and the missing transverse momentum vector to suppress the dominant backgrounds. Polarization-sensitive observables built from the hadronic $τ$ decay products are also examined as complementary probes of the spin-$0$ origin of the $τ$ leptons. The expected discovery sensitivity is evaluated using the Asimov significance for an integrated luminosity of $3$ ab$^{-1}$ at $\sqrt{s}=14$ TeV. Our results demonstrate that the $2τ\:+\:2b\:+$ missing $E_T$ channel provides a promising and largely orthogonal avenue to search for non-standard VLQ decays in extended Higgs sectors, with discovery-level sensitivity achievable for VLQ masses up to approximately $1.9$ TeV.

Abstract: We present a simple Dirac scoto-seesaw framework based on the anomaly-free $U(1)_{B-L}$ charge assignment $(-4,-4,5)$ for $ν_R$. After the spontaneous breaking of gauged $U(1)_{B-L}$, a residual $Z_6$ symmetry stabilizes the dark matter candidate. We explore the dark matter phenomenology of the singlet scalar and fermionic dark matter candidates. While singlet scalar DM is often severely constrained, the presence of the $Z'$ portal together with annihilation and co-annihilation channels substantially broadens the allowed parameter space. Thus, the framework offers a predictive scenario for neutrino and dark matter phenomenology that can be probed in future experiments.

Abstract: We investigate the first-order phase transition that terminates thermal inflation and evaluate the associated stochastic gravitational-wave signals. The transition is first characterized through semi-analytic calculations of the bounce action, which are compared with numerical results obtained using CosmoTransitions. We then study its real-time evolution in a three-dimensional Langevin lattice simulation that incorporates Hubble expansion and the corresponding temperature evolution throughout the transition. The lattice dynamics are consistent with the bounce-action estimates: the transition proceeds through localized bubble nucleation and subsequent bubble growth, rather than through a phase-mixing instability. Using the resulting transition parameters, we estimate the gravitational-wave spectra generated by bubble collisions and acoustic motions in the plasma. The predicted stochastic background lies within the projected sensitivity ranges of future gravitational-wave observatories, including BBO and DECIGO.

Conclusion: 模型修改对EAS观测量有显著影响，需通过加速器数据约束以减小宇宙线成分分析中的系统误差。

Abstract: A new Monte Carlo generator of hadronic collisions, QGSb, is applied for studying model uncertainties regarding calculations of the development of extensive air showers (EAS) initiated by interactions of high energy cosmic rays in the atmosphere. More specifically, we investigate possibilities to modify the model predictions for two EAS characteristics mostly used in experimental studies of cosmic ray composition: air shower maximum depth and the muon number at ground level. For all the considered modifications of the model, we discuss in some detail the underlying physics mechanisms and investigate the impact of the changes, regarding a comparison of the model results to relevant accelerator data.

</details>


### [97] [Three-particle di-light-cone distribution amplitudes of the $B$-meson in heavy-quark effective theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20267)

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了B介子的三粒子双光锥分布振幅（DLCDAs），定义了背靠背光线上反夸克和胶子场强张量的三局域HQET算符矩阵元，推导了完整的洛伦兹分解，识别出8个独立DLCDAs并按扭度分类，利用局域算符恒等式和运动方程约束获得了树级归一化积分和一阶矩关系，构建了动量空间模型，并在领头扭度处引入了α_s阶辐射修正。

Conclusion: 这些结果为非因子化软胶子贡献的非微扰动力学提供了系统参数化方案，可用于改进稀有和非轻子B介子衰变的唯象学研究，其中领头扭度的辐射修正确保了模型在微扰能标下的自洽性。

Abstract: We present a systematic study of the three-particle di-light-cone distribution amplitudes (DLCDAs) of the $B$-meson. They are defined through $B$-meson--to--vacuum matrix elements of trilocal HQET operators, in which the light antiquark and the gluon field-strength tensor are located on two back-to-back light rays. In this sense, the DLCDAs generalise the conventional $B$-meson light-cone distribution amplitudes to configurations where soft fields couple to collinear degrees of freedom in two distinct directions. As such, they parametrise the non-perturbative dynamics associated with non-factorisable soft-gluon contributions in rare and non-leptonic exclusive $B$-meson decays. We derive the complete Lorentz decomposition of the matrix elements of generic trilocal operators, identify eight independent DLCDAs, and organise them in a basis of definite twist. Using local operator identities and equations-of-motion constraints, we obtain tree-level relations for their normalisation integrals and first moments in terms of a minimal set of hadronic parameters. These relations allow us to construct simple momentum-space models for all independent DLCDAs. For the leading-twist distribution, we further incorporate the perturbative radiative tail at order $α_s$ and discuss its impact on the resulting parametrisation.

### [98] [String Axiverse Enhancement of Superradiant Dark Matter Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20524)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究弦理论预言的大量轻轴子物种对原初黑洞通过蒸发和超辐射产生暗物质过程的影响，特别是这些轴子如何改变超辐射效率以及暗物质形成的参数空间。

Method: 理论分析：研究弦轴子（约100-10⁵种）对原初黑洞蒸发和超辐射过程的综合影响，分析轴子种类数量与黑洞自旋、蒸发速率、超辐射云质量之间的关联，并评估对宇宙学观测（如复合时期相对论性自由度）的影响。

Result: 弦轴子显著增强超辐射效率，扩大暗物质以微玻色子星形式存在的参数空间；但轴子种类过多会导致PBH蒸发过快，阻碍超辐射云达到最大质量；PBH蒸发产生的轴子对复合时期ΔN_eff贡献可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 弦轴子对PBH产生暗物质的过程有重要影响，既扩大了微玻色子星作为暗物质的可行参数区域，又受到轴子种类数目的限制。该研究为弦轴子暗物质场景提供了可检验的宇宙学预言。

Abstract: We study the effects of string axion emission on dark matter production by light primordial black holes (PBHs), through both evaporation and superradiance. We show, in particular, that the Hawking emission of $\mathcal{O}(100-10^5)$ light axion species predicted in realistic string theory constructions can significantly enhance the efficiency of superradiance, given the associated increase in the PBH spin. The string axiverse thus significantly expands the parametric regions (dark matter mass and PBH mass and spin) for which a sizeable fraction of dark matter may presently be in the form of ``micro-boson stars'': the self-gravitating remnants of superradiant dark matter clouds. Conversely, for too large a number of axion species PBHs evaporate too quickly for superradiant clouds to attain their maximum mass. Finally, assuming that all dark matter is produced by PBHs (through both superradiance and Hawking emission), we show that the axions emitted during PBH evaporation give an immeasurably small contribution to the relativistic degrees of freedom at recombination.

### [99] [Dyonic lattices, $θ$-angles and axions in the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20319)

Conclusion: 标准模型的θ参数空间具有丰富的结构，Witten效应与全局规范群结构紧密相关；电磁单极子的电荷测量可提供标准模型参数的额外约束；axion物理需要更复杂的框架才能实现完全的CP不变性。

Abstract: We investigate the implications of the Witten effect in the Standard Model with a general global gauge group structure and determine the values of the three $θ$-parameters that lead to distinct families of allowed spectra of dyons. We construct and classify the corresponding dyonic charge lattices consistent with the Standard Model gauge structure. This approach enables us to re-derive the known global-group--dependent periodicities of the $θ$ angles and to determine all CP-invariant points in $θ$-space. The electromagnetic subgroup $U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$ is shown to arise \emph{prior} to electroweak symmetry breaking by factoring out the effect of the anomalous $B+L$ transformations, which reduces the physical $θ$-parameter space from a three-torus to a two-torus. Our phenomenological conclusions include an observation that a discovery of a $U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$ monopole carrying non-zero electric charge would determine the last remaining unknown parameter of the Standard Model. Lastly we study how $θ$-space shapes axion physics with emphasis on the axion-photon coupling and show that a single axion is insufficient to render the Standard Model vacuum fully CP invariant.

### [100] [Theory Calculations for LDMX and LOHENGRIN beyond Coherent Bethe-Heitler Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20327)

They aim to search for missing momentum signals sourced by the direct production of dark photons with masses in the MeV-GeV range in bremsstrahlung processes, in which an electron beam of a few GeV scatters off a fixed target. So far, the signal characteristics, i.e. the behavior of the recoiling electron, have mostly been studied in coherent Bethe-Heitler electron-nucleus scattering with a dark photon that couples only to the Standard Model charged leptons. In this work, we present the calculations of the differential cross sections of all contributing real emission processes up to third order in the electromagnetic fine structure constant and fourth order in the kinetic mixing parameter associated with the dark photon. We consider a dark photon coupling to both the beam electron and the hadronic target and we take into account the scattering off both the target nucleus and its nuclear constituents. Besides real emission processes, we also discuss virtual dark photon contributions and their relevance for the signal prediction. After discussing the different phase space regions and constraints emerging from the experimental setups, we show numerical results of the cross sections and differential distributions, including the signal and dominant background. Within our framework, we find that the LOHENGRIN experiment will require an extension of its HCAL to effectively veto background processes originating from diffractive scattering. Apart from that, the contributions beyond coherent Bethe-Heitler scattering, in the presence of realistic experimental selections, have only a limited effect on the predicted signal and background in the relevant dark photon mass range.

### [103] [New Gauge Forces, Neutron Stars and Schwinger Neutrino Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20393)
*Yuxin Liu,Zhen Liu,Andrey Shkerin,Jing Shu,Yue Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了由$B-L$、$L_e-L_{μ/τ}$或$L_μ-L_τ$规范对称性产生的新长程力对中微子的影响。天体产生的轻子势会导致带电中微子的Schwinger对产生。对于$L_μ-L_τ$力，在耦合常数$g\gtrsim 10^{-18}$时，中子星中的效应显著：改变元素丰度并抑制电荷，从而推翻来自中子星并合的约束。Schwinger效应产生的中微子通量可能被距离$\simeq 100$ pc的年轻中子星探测到，典型能量$E_ν\sim 100$ MeV，专门搜索可将约束重新确立为$g\lesssim 10^{-18}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索由轻子数规范对称性产生的新长程力对中微子的影响，特别是天体产生的轻子势如何导致中微子的Schwinger对产生，以及这些效应对不同对称性($B-L$、$L_e-L_{μ/τ}$、$L_μ-L_τ$)下的可观测性和现有约束的影响。

Method: 理论分析天体（地球、太阳、中子星）产生的轻子势对带电中微子的影响，计算Schwinger对产生机制下中微子的产生率、累积形成的简并费米气体以及逃逸粒子形成的稳态中微子通量，并评估不同规范对称性和耦合强度下的可观测性。

Result: 对于$B-L$和$L_e-L_{μ/τ}$力，效应太弱无法观测。对于$L_μ-L_τ$力，当$g\gtrsim 10^{-18}$时在中子星中效应显著：改变平衡态元素丰度，抑制$L_μ-L_τ$电荷，从而推翻来自中子星并合的约束($g\gtrsim 10^{-17}$)。当$g\gtrsim 10^{-18}$时，Schwinger效应产生的中微子通量可能从距离$\simeq 100$ pc的单个年轻中子星被探测到，典型能量$E_ν\sim 100$ MeV。

Conclusion: 对$L_μ-L_τ$力的专门中微子信号搜索可将耦合常数约束重新确立为$g\lesssim 10^{-18}$，这比从中子星并合得到的约束更强。

Abstract: We investigate neutrino effects of new long-range forces arising from gauging $B-L$, $L_e-L_{μ/τ}$ or $L_μ-L_τ$ symmetries of the Standard Model. The leptonic potential generated by astronomical bodies, such as the Earth, the Sun or a neutron star, results in the Schwinger pair production of neutrinos charged under the new gauge symmetry. The oppositely charged particles accumulate in the potential well forming a degenerate Fermi gas, while equally charged particles fly away forming a steady flux of neutrinos. We find that, for the $B-L$ and $L_e-L_{μ/τ}$ forces, these effects are too weak to be observable. For the $L_μ-L_τ$ force these effects are significant in neutron stars if the gauge coupling is $g\gtrsim 10^{-18}$. The muonic force changes the element abundances of a neutron star in equilibrium and suppresses its $L_μ-L_τ$ charge. This invalidates the constraint on $g$ from neutron star mergers, at $g\gtrsim 10^{-17}$. Furthermore, for such values of $g$, the neutrino flux produced by the Schwinger effect could potentially be detected from a single young neutron star at a distance of $\simeq 100$ pc, with the typical neutrino energy $E_ν\sim 100$ MeV. A dedicated search for such a signal will reassert the bound $g\lesssim 10^{-18}$.

*Raoul Serao,Aniello Quaranta,Antonio Capolupo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: X17粒子若被证实，将标志着超出标准模型的新物理，但当前证据仍需进一步实验验证；未来实验方向将有助于确认或排除其存在。

Abstract: This review summarizes the experimental evidence for the hypothetical X17 particle, examines the theoretical frameworks in which it can be accommodated, and discusses its potential implications for the Standard Model and couplings to known particles. Future experimental prospects are also highlighted.

</details>


### [105] [The $B^+ \to K^+ ν\bar ν$ decay as a QCD axion search: comparing reinterpretation approaches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20525)
*Merna Abumusabh,Giulio Dujany,Diego Guadagnoli,Méril Reboud,Claudio Toni*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 对Belle II $B^+ \to K^+\nu\bar\nu$数据的两种分析因运动学变量选择导致$B^+ \to K^+ a$分支比上限相差约四倍；基于$q^2_{\rm rec}$的精细分箱能有效分辨轴子信号，而基于BDT的似然因与$q^2$不相关而缺乏区分力；提倡实验合作在发布BDT似然的同时公开物理变量空间的似然投影以增强可重解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阐明Belle II数据中两种分析方法对$B^+ \to K^+ a$分支比上限产生显著差异的原因，并评估基于$q^2_{\rm rec}$方法的保守性及BDT方法的局限性。

Method: 对比不同运动学变量空间（$q^2_{\rm rec}$精细分箱 vs. $q^2_{\rm rec}\times\eta({\rm BDT}_2)$空间）的灵敏度；通过数值测试验证BDT轴与$q^2$的不相关性；引入亚主导形状系统误差评估方法的保守性。

Result: $q^2_{\rm rec}$的精细分箱能有效分辨窄轴子信号，而粗分箱会稀释信号；BDT轴对$B^+ \to K^+ a$几乎无区分力；亚主导形状系统误差进一步降低上限，使$q^2_{\rm rec}$方法更保守；运动学轴选择本身即可解释约四倍的灵敏度差异。

Conclusion: BDT主导的似然在信号形状与训练信号差异较大时重解释价值有限；建议实验合作方同时发布物理变量空间与BDT空间的似然投影以最大化测量的可重解释性。

Abstract: Two recent independent analyses of Belle II $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ data yield limits on ${\mathcal B}(B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a)$ -- the two-body mode to a light invisible particle such as the QCD axion -- differing by a factor of roughly four; we trace this to the choice of kinematic variable space. The central figure of merit is the resolution in the reconstructed di-neutrino invariant mass $q^2_{\rm rec}$: fine-grained binning resolves the narrow axion signal, while coarse binning dilutes it into a background-dominated range. A BDT axis trained on $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ adds little discriminating power for $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$, as this axis is largely uncorrelated with $q^2$. These expectations are confirmed by a set of numerical tests. The subleading shape systematics omitted from our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based approach {\em lower}, not raise, the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$ limit: by better accommodating the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ shape, they leave less room for the axion signal, making our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based bound conservative, if anything. A dedicated reanalysis confirms that the kinematic-axes choice alone accounts for the factor-of-four sensitivity difference, and that the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$ bound varies sizeably within the $q^2_{\rm rec}\timesη({\rm BDT}_2)$ space, depending on the SM-likeness of $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$, thus losing the dual-probe feature of our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based approach. These results point to a broader consideration: likelihoods dominated by BDT variables are of limited use for reinterpretations when the signal shape differs appreciably from the BDT's training signal. We therefore advocate that experimental collaborations publish likelihood projections in physical variable spaces alongside BDT-based likelihoods, to maximise the reinterpretability of their measurements.

</details>


### [106] [Rotating magnetized pion gas of finite transverse size: condensation constraints and transport properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20530)
*Ankit Kumar,Diwakar Gaur,Vinod Chandra*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在背景磁场中，具有有限横向半径的旋转π介子气体的电、热和热电响应，发现磁场与旋转之间存在竞争关系：磁场抑制输运系数，而旋转（作为有效化学势）促进其增强，超过临界角速度后旋转增强效应压倒磁抑制效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究旋转和磁场共同作用下π介子气体的输运特性，特别是两者对电导率、热导率和塞贝克系数的竞争性影响机制。

Method: 采用弛豫时间近似下的玻尔兹曼输运方程，计算纵向电导率、热导率和塞贝克系数；明确π⁺凝聚的参数边界并确保工作区间安全远离该边界。

Result: 发现凝聚不对称性（π⁺凝聚而π⁻未凝聚）；磁场抑制而旋转（作为有效化学势）增强输运系数；超过临界角速度后旋转增强效应超越磁抑制效应；通过洛伦兹数分析了电荷与热输运的相对重要性。

Conclusion: 旋转效应对旋转磁化π介子介质的输运性质有显著影响，其作为有效化学势引入的能量偏移可逆转型磁场的抑制效应，为理解强场旋转系统（如重离子碰撞）中的输运现象提供了新见解。

Abstract: This work investigates the electric, thermal, and thermoelectric responses of a rotating pion gas of finite transverse radius in the presence of a background magnetic field, with the rotation axis aligned with the magnetic field. We explicitly calculate the parameter limits for $π^+$ condensation and restrict our working regime safely outside these boundaries, ensuring well-behaved transport coefficients. Notably, the system exhibits a condensation asymmetry, with $π^-$ remaining uncondensed at the parameters that induce $π^+$ condensation. Using the Boltzmann Transport Equation under the Relaxation Time Approximation, we calculate the longitudinal electrical conductivity, thermal conductivity, and the Seebeck coefficient. Our results reveal a competing interplay between the magnetic field and rotation, highlighting the substantial impact of rotation on the medium's transport properties: while the magnetic field suppresses the transport coefficients in a static medium, rotation, acting as an effective chemical potential, introduces an energy shift that favors their increase. Beyond an angular velocity, this rotational enhancement overpowers the magnetic suppression, leading to an increase in the transport coefficients with increasing magnetic field. Finally, we analyze the relative significance of charge and heat transport through the Lorenz number, providing further insight into the transport characteristics of the rotating magnetized pion medium.

</details>

### [107] [Geometric Rigidity via Harmonic Twisted Spinors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19567)
*Francesco Bei,Simone Cecchini*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文利用Gromov精确提升闭二形式方法，在闭黎曼自旋流形上证明了若存在同调非平凡的闭二形式，且其提升到万有覆盖是恰当的，则成立尖锐的双曲标量曲率比较定理（与万有黎曼覆盖谱底相关）。通过Gromov扭曲L²指标产生调和旋量，并分析等式情形，证明原度量是爱因斯坦的；在正谱情形下，万有覆盖为实双曲空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Gromov的精确提升闭二形式方法推广到标量曲率几何中，建立标量曲率与万有覆盖谱底之间的尖锐比较，并刻画等式情形的几何刚性。

Method: 利用Gromov扭曲L²指标定理，通过一族小酉扭曲产生调和旋量；结合精细Kato等式缺陷的共形解释，用调和旋量构造相对于共形度量平行的旋量。

Result: 证明了尖锐的双曲标量曲率比较定理；在等式情形下，原始度量是爱因斯坦度量；正谱情形下万有覆盖为实双曲空间。

Conclusion: Gromov的精确提升闭二形式方法在标量曲率几何中有效，能够导出尖锐的曲率比较与刚性分类结果，为标量曲率与谱几何的联系提供了新工具。

Abstract: We study Gromov's exact-lift two-form method in scalar-curvature geometry. For a closed Riemannian spin manifold carrying a homologically non-trivial closed two-form whose lift to the universal cover is exact, we prove the sharp hyperbolic scalar-curvature comparison with the bottom of the spectrum of the universal Riemannian covering. The two-form enters through Gromov's twisted \(L^2\)-index, which produces harmonic spinors for a family of small unitary twists. We analyze the equality case by interpreting the refined Kato equality defect conformally and use the harmonic spinors to construct a parallel spinor with respect to a suitable conformally related metric. This yields that the original metric is Einstein. In the positive-spectrum case, this method implies that the universal cover is real hyperbolic.

### [108] [Some constructions of uniformly positive scalar curvature metrics on open manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19619)
*Anushree Das*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文给出了在开流形上构造一致正数量曲率完备黎曼度量的若干结果。对于维数n≥3，若流形存在有界下方的适当Morse函数且无指数≥n-2的临界点，或存在正数量曲率度量及每个边界为极小的紧穷竭，则存在一致正数量曲率度量。对于4≤n≤7，若流形具有乘积端及C-二次衰减（C>4π²）的正数量曲率度量，则存在足够远的平均凸超曲面蕴含一致正数量曲率度量。应用包括：无一致正数量曲率度量的流形若具有平均凸穷竭，则存在紧集的平均凸叶状结构；若具有平均凹穷竭，则其端具有平均凹叶状结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究开流形上一致正数量曲率度量的存在性问题，这是正曲率几何中的重要课题。一致正数量曲率比普通正数量曲率更强的条件，其存在性条件更苛刻。

Method: 利用Morse理论分析临界点指数条件；利用极小边界穷竭构造；利用二次衰减条件下的平均凸超曲面构造；通过叶状结构分析推广。

Result: 给出了三种不同条件下一致正数量曲率度量的存在性定理，以及正/负曲率流形末端叶状结构的刻画。

Conclusion: 建立了开流形上一致正数量曲率度量存在的充分条件，并揭示了平均凸/凹穷竭与叶状结构之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We obtain several constructions of uniformly positive scalar curvature complete Riemannian metrics on open manifolds. For dimension $n\geq3$, we show that if such a manifold admits a proper Morse function $f$ bounded below such that $f$ has no critical points of index $\geq n-2$, then it admits a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric. On the other hand if such a manifold admits a positive scalar curvature metric along with a compact exhaustion $\{U_i\}$ such that the boundary of each $U_i$ is minimal, then it also admits a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric. For dimension $4 \leq n\leq 7$, we show that if the manifold has product ends and a positive scalar curvature metric with $C$-quadratic decay at infinity for $C>4π^2$ with respect to some basepoint, then the existence of a mean convex hypersurface far enough from the basepoint implies the existence of a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric on the manifold. We study some applications of these results, including showing that if an open manifold of dimension $n\geq 3$ that admits no uniformly positive scalar curvature metric has a positive scalar curvature metric with mean convex exhaustion, then it admits a mean convex foliation of compact sets sufficiently close to the ends. On the other hand, if such a manifold has a mean concave exhaustion, then its ends admit a mean concave foliation.

</details>

Method: 引入多复变或CR几何中的质量概念，通过CR-Sobolev商寻找Yamabe问题的极小化子，利用正质量定理求解正曲率情形下具有最小能量的Yamabe方程。

Result: 在3维CR几何中建立了正质量定理，研究了Rossi球面的CR-Sobolev商，并将理论推广到5维情形。

Conclusion: 正质量定理在CR几何的Yamabe问题中起关键作用，为寻找正曲率情形下具有最小能量的Yamabe方程解提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Our goal is to survey the development of positive mass theorem and the Yamabe equation on CR manifolds in recent years. We introduce the notion of the mass in several complex variables or CR geometry. We then consider the Yamabe problem on CR manifolds to find a minimizer for the CR-Sobolev quotient. The positive mass theorem plays a key role in finding a solution to the Yamabe equation with minimum energy for the positive curvature case. We mainly focus on the team works in the following three papers [CMY17], [CMY23] and [CC22], on a positive mass theorem in 3-dimensional CR geometry, the CR-Sobolev quotient of Rossi spheres, and the 5-dimensional situation, respectively.

### [110] [The top Yau--Yang conjecture for Kähler manifolds with positive sectional curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19806)

Method: 主要方法包括：(1) 利用Bézout估计技术；(2) 构造具有有限Monge-Ampère质量的Lipschitz权函数；(3) 结合Chen-Zhu的已有结果。

Result: 证明了正截面曲率完备非紧Kähler流形的Ricci形式顶楔积分为有限值；在截面曲率有界条件下，此类流形是拟射影的。

Conclusion: 正截面曲率完备非紧Kähler流形具有重要的几何有限性性质，且在曲率有界条件下具有拟射影性，这为理解这类流形的代数几何结构提供了新见解。

Abstract: We prove that the top wedge power of the Ricci form of a complete non-compact Kähler manifold with positive sectional curvature has finite integral. A key new idea to prove Bézout estimates along with a Lipschitz weight with finite Monge-Ampère mass is used in the proof of the main result.

### [112] [Poisson and Jacobi structures from 2-covariant tensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20030)
*Manuel de León,Xavier Gràcia,Rubén Izquierdo-López,Ángel Martínez-Muñoz,Xavier Rivas*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一框架，通过研究由非退化2-协变张量诱导的Poisson和Jacobi结构，推导了Schouten-Nijenhuis括号的计算公式，并用曲率和外微分表示了该括号，从而给出了Poisson或Jacobi结构存在的障碍。该框架统一了辛、局部共形辛、余辛和接触几何中的经典括号，并刻画了胖丛和p阶殆余辛结构确定Jacobi括号的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Poisson和Jacobi结构在经典力学的几何描述中具有基础性作用，但通常由非退化2-协变张量诱导的双向量场对应的括号缺乏统一的构造框架。本文旨在建立这样的统一框架，并通过曲率等几何量刻画结构存在的障碍。

Method: 在张量的适当假设下，推导了关联双向量场的Schouten-Nijenhuis括号用某分布的曲率和微分形式的外微分表示的计算公式，该公式提供了Poisson或Jacobi结构存在的障碍条件。通过该框架统一恢复了辛、局部共形辛、余辛和接触几何中的经典括号，并进一步刻画了胖丛和p阶殆余辛结构确定Jacobi括号的条件。

Result: 得到了Schouten-Nijenhuis括号的曲率-外微分表示公式，该公式给出了Poisson/Jacobi结构存在的障碍。成功用统一框架恢复了辛、局部共形辛、余辛和接触几何的经典括号。给出了胖丛和p阶殆余辛结构成为Jacobi结构的充要条件。

Conclusion: 本文建立的统一框架有效统一了多种经典几何结构中的括号构造，其障碍条件具有清晰的几何解释（曲率与外微分），为更广泛几何系统中Poisson和Jacobi结构的研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: Poisson and Jacobi structures play a fundamental role in the geometric description of many systems arising in classical mechanics. In most cases, the corresponding bivector field is induced by a non-degenerate 2-covariant tensor. In this paper, we present a unified framework for constructing the associated brackets by studying the Poisson and Jacobi structures induced by these tensors. More specifically, under suitable assumptions on the tensor, we derive a formula for computing the Schouten-Nijenhuis bracket of the associated bivector field in terms of the curvature of a certain distribution and the exterior derivative of a differential form. This formula provides the obstruction to the existence of a Poisson or Jacobi structure. To illustrate the theory, we recover the classical brackets associated with symplectic, locally conformally symplectic, cosymplectic, and contact geometries. Finally, we characterize the conditions under which fat bundles and almost cosymplectic structures of order $p$ determine a Jacobi bracket.

</details>


### [113] [Comparison Theorems for the Profile Curve Equation of Rotationally Symmetric Self-Shrinkers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20276)
*Peng Peng*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文从常微分方程角度研究旋转对称自收缩子，通过分析垂直点轨迹的交集给出Angenent环面存在性的新证明，并推导线性化方程，利用Sturm型比较定理得到水平点轨迹单调性的充分条件，为Angenent环面的唯一性问题提供了可能的研究途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Angenent环面是平均曲率流中最重要的紧致自收缩例子之一，但其唯一性是一个长期未解决的重要公开问题。

Method: 将旋转对称自收缩子问题转化为常微分方程，分析轮廓曲线的垂直点及其轨迹；推导线性化方程并应用Sturm型比较定理研究水平点轨迹的单调性。

Result: 给出了Angenent环面存在性的新证明；得到了球面自收缩子附近解的比较定理；建立了水平点轨迹的部分单调性结果。

Conclusion: 这些结果为证明Angenent环面的唯一性提供了可能的研究途径。

Abstract: Mean curvature flow is a fundamental geometric evolution equation in which a submanifold moves in the normal direction with velocity equal to its mean curvature vector. Self-shrinkers arise naturally as self-similar solutions to the mean curvature flow and play an important role as models for finite-time singularities. Among nontrivial examples of compact embedded self-shrinkers, the rotationally symmetric self-shrinking torus constructed by Angenent is one of the most important. However, the uniqueness of the Angenent torus remains a major open problem.
  In this paper, we study rotationally symmetric self-shrinkers of type $\mathbb{S}^{1}\times \mathbb{S}^{n-1}$ from the point of view of ordinary differential equations. We analyze the profile curves of rotationally symmetric self-shrinkers, focusing on the behavior of their vertical points and the curves traced out by these points as the initial height varies. We give a new proof of the existence of the Angenent torus by showing that two families of vertical-point trajectories must intersect.
  We further derive the linearized equation associated with the rotationally symmetric self-shrinker equation and apply a Sturm-type comparison theorem to obtain sufficient conditions for the monotonicity of horizontal-point trajectories. In particular, we prove a comparison theorem for solutions near the spherical self-shrinker $x^{2}+r^{2}=2n$, and establish partial monotonicity results for the curves of horizontal points. These results provide a possible approach to the uniqueness problem for the Angenent torus.

</details>


### [114] [The Hermitian-Yang-Mills Iteration on Stable Bundles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20307)
*Huai-Dong Cao,Xiaofeng Sun,Shing-Tung Yau,Yingying Zhang*

Abstract: In this paper, based on recent results for the prescribed Hermitian-Yang-Mills (HYM) tensor and its twisted variants by Fan-Wang-Yang-Yau, we provide a dynamical construction of Hermitian-Einstein metrics on stable holomorphic vector bundles and its extension to Higgs bundles. ### [115] [The alignment time function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20481)
*Marco van den Beld-Serrano*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究在稳定因果时空中，给定一个过去指向的类时向量场，是否存在一个时间函数使其梯度与该向量场最优对齐。通过引入一个衡量错位并惩罚零梯度的泛函，证明了在适当条件下存在唯一的光滑时间函数（称为对齐时间函数），并建立了其陡度改善、稳定性及对称性继承等性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决一个基础性问题：给定固定的过去指向类时向量场，是否存在一个时间函数，其梯度与该向量场达到最优对齐？

Method: 引入一个泛函，该泛函一方面衡量类时向量场与Sobolev函数梯度之间的错位，另一方面惩罚零梯度。在光滑稳定因果时空的紧致子集上，在合适的Sobolev指数和零梯度惩罚强度假设下，证明存在唯一的光滑时间函数最小化该泛函。

Result: 证明了存在唯一的光滑时间函数（对齐时间函数）最小化所考虑的泛函；该函数具有可规范改善陡度、在C^p收敛下对底层度规和向量场稳定、继承度规和给定向量场的对称性等性质。

Conclusion: 成功构建了对齐时间函数，并建立了其重要性质，为时空结构中时间函数与向量场的对齐问题提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Given a fixed past-directed timelike vector field, does there exist a time function whose gradient is optimally aligned with it? We address this question by introducing a functional that, on the one hand, captures the misalignment between the timelike vector field and the gradients of suitable Sobolev functions, and, on the other hand, penalizes null gradients. Our analysis focuses on compact subsets of smooth stably causal spacetimes. More precisely, we prove that, under suitable assumptions on the Sobolev index and the strength of the null gradient penalization, there exists a unique smooth temporal function which minimizes the considered functional. We refer to this minimizer as the \emph{alignment time function}. Furthermore, several useful properties of the alignment time function are established: there exists a canonical procedure to improve its steepness, it is stable under $C^{p}$ convergence of the underlying metrics and vector fields and it inherits the symmetries shared by the metric and the given vector field.

</details>

We give a numerically stable method for recovering the 11 parameters from a given elastic curve segment. Using this, we give a fast and stable method to approximate an arbitrary space curve segment by a 3D elastica. Abstract: In light of recent advances in conformal blow-up methods for the positive mass theorem, including He--Shi--Yu, Bi--Hao--He--Shi--Zhu, and Brendle--Wang, we develop a Schoen--Yau type singular dimension descent method for positive scalar curvature obstructions in arbitrary dimensions. ### [118] [Lagrangian capacity and chain level string topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20051)
*Shah Faisal,Yin Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Cieliebak-Mohnke关于椭球Lagrangian容量的猜想，建立任意维凸/凹环面域Lagrangian容量的一般理论，并克服使用带局部切触约束的全纯曲线导致的横截性问题。

Method: 发展Fukaya-Irie技术的S^1-等变变体，避免使用带局部切触约束的全纯曲线；利用Gutt-Hutchings容量建立上界。

Result: 证明了凸或凹环面域的Lagrangian容量等于其对角线；椭球中极值Lagrangian环面必在边界上；给出了Liouville流形中非球面Lagrangian宽度新上界；首次计算了4维和6维非次临界Weinstein域的Lagrangian容量。

Conclusion: 完全解决了Cieliebak-Mohnke猜想，为Lagrangian容量的计算提供了新方法，拓展了在更高维度和非次临界情形下的应用。

Abstract: We derive upper bounds for the Lagrangian capacities of Liouville domains with finite Gutt--Hutchings capacities and show that the Lagrangian capacity of a convex or concave toric domain of arbitrary dimension equals its diagonal. In particular, this completely settles the conjecture of Cieliebak-Mohnke on the Lagrangian capacity of ellipsoids. Our proof is based on an $S^1$-equivariant variant of the techniques of Fukaya and Irie, and does not use holomorphic curves with local tangency constraints, which would inevitably cause transversality issues. Moreover, we show that any extremal Lagrangian torus in an $n$-dimensional ellipsoid must lie on the boundary. Applications of our results and techniques include new upper bounds on the Lagrangian width for aspherical Lagrangians in Liouville manifolds and the first computations of the Lagrangian capacities for many non-subcritical Weinstein domains in dimensions 4 and 6.

### [119] [Fourier-Helgason transform as infinite geodesic time limit in geometric quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20290)
*Ana Cristina Ferreira,Joachim Hilgert,José M. Mourão,João P. Nunes*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文解决了对于非紧对称空间 $G/K$，当 $G$ 为非复李群时，Fourier-Helgason 变换与几何量子化（BKS 配对）之间的不一致性。通过引入 geodesic flow 的无穷时间极限，构造了量子测地线变换（QGT），并证明其极限等于 FH 变换（相差 Harish-Chandra $c$-函数的相位和一个常数因子）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lisiecki (1987) 对复李群 $G$ 给出了 FH 变换的几何量子化解释，但发现对于非复李群，BKS 配对与 FH 变换不等价且非酉。本文旨在解决这一不一致性。

Method: 1. 证明水平极化是 $G$-不变黎曼度量的测地流作用下垂直极化的无穷时间极限。
2. 将测地流提升为量子丛上的酉平行输运，称为量子测地线变换（QGT）。
3. 证明 QGT 在测地时间趋于无穷时存在极限，且该极限等于 FH 变换（相差 Harish-Chandra $c$-函数相位和常数因子）。

Result: QGT 的无穷时间极限与 FH 变换等价，从而桥接了非复李群情形下几何量子化与调和分析之间的鸿沟。

Conclusion: 通过量子测地线变换，成功将几何量子化框架应用于非复 Lie 群的 FH 变换，解决了长期存在的不一致性问题。

Abstract: The Fourier-Helgason (FH) transform for a noncompact symmetric space $G/K$ establishes the direct integral decomposition of the unitary representation of $G$ on $L^2(G/K)$ into irreducible principal series representations.
  By applying techniques of geometric quantization to the symplectic manifold $T^*(G/K),$ Lisiecki in 1987 gave a geometric interpretation of the FH transform in the case when $G$ is complex. He defined for general $G$ a ''horizontal'' polarization on $T^*(G/K)$ and showed that, for complex $G$, the Blattner-Kostant-Sternberg (BKS) pairing between the Schrödinger vertical polarization Hilbert space, $L^2(G/K)$, and the Hilbert space of horizontally polarized functions coincides with the FH transform. However, in the same paper, Lisiecki showed that for noncomplex Lie groups the BKS pairing is nonequivalent to the FH transform and nonunitary in general.
  In the present paper, we resolve this discrepancy between the FH transform and geometric quantization in the case when $G$ is not complex.
  First, we show that the horizontal polarization is the infinite-time limit of the push-forward of the vertical polarization with respect to the geodesic flow for a $G$-invariant Riemannian metric. Then we lift the geodesic flow to an intertwining unitary parallel transport on the quantum bundle that we call quantum geodesic transform (QGT). Finally we show that the QGT has a well-defined limit, as the geodesic time goes to infinity, and that it is equal, up to the phase of the Harish-Chandra $c$-function and an irrelevant multiplicative constant, to the FH transform.

</details>

### [120] [Bootstrapping Pion Form Factors at Large $N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19420)
*Jan Albert,Dilara Kosva,Leonardo Rastelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在大N QCD框架下，对π介子形状因子进行自举研究，利用解析性、幺正性及Regge有界性等谱数据约束，得到了两类界限：一是基于解析性和Brodsky-Farrar标度律的严格普适界限，二是类似SVZ求和规则的唯象界限，从而将手征拉格朗日参数空间压缩至大N QCD预期区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立从强子自举到微观QCD拉格朗日量之间的规范桥接，通过大N QCD中π介子形状因子的自举研究，探索局部规范不变探针如何连接低能强子物理与QCD的微扰紫外行为。

Method: 考虑大N极限下矢量流两点函数、π介子矢量形状因子和π介子散射振幅的混合系统，利用谱数据的亚纯性、幺正性、交叉对称性和Regge有界性，结合解析性、幺正性及Brodsky-Farrar渐近标度律导出严格界限；同时通过输入有限能标处的微扰紫外行为，导出类似SVZ求和规则的唯象界限。

Result: 得到了两类界限：第一类是严格且普适的，约束了低能形状因子系数；第二类是唯象的，可以约束π介子衰变常数、将大N格点测量转换为渐近自由能标的下界、以及约束π介子电荷半径。综合这些输入，手征拉格朗日的允许参数空间被压缩至大N QCD预期区域。

Conclusion: 局部规范不变探针为强子自举与微观QCD拉格朗日量之间提供了标准桥梁，展示了在QCD中结合解析性、幺正性和渐近行为进行系统性自举研究的可行性与有效性。

Abstract: We initiate a bootstrap study of pion form factors in large $N$ QCD. We consider the mixed system of the vector-current two-point function, the pion vector form factor, and the pion scattering amplitude in the chiral limit. At large $N$ these observables are meromorphic, with spectral data constrained by unitarity, crossing symmetry, and Regge boundedness. We obtain bounds of two kinds. The first are rigorous and universal: from analyticity, unitarity and the asymptotic Brodsky-Farrar scaling, we constrain low-energy form-factor coefficients. The second are more phenomenological, of the Shifman-Vainshtein-Zakharov type: feeding in the perturbative ultraviolet behavior at a finite scale lets us bound the pion decay constant, convert a large $N$ lattice measurement into a lower bound on the scale at which asymptotic freedom sets in, and constrain the pion charge radius. Combining these inputs, the space of allowed chiral Lagrangians shrinks toward the region where large $N$ QCD is expected to sit. Our results illustrate how local gauge-invariant probes provide a canonical bridge between the hadronic bootstrap and the microscopic QCD Lagrangian.

### [122] [Moduli Stabilisation for ADD and the Dark Dimension Scenario](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19440)
*Andreas P. Braun,Michele Cicoli,Riccardo Milioli,Roberto Valandro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在IIB型大体积弦紧化框架下，通过K3纤维化的Calabi-Yau三折叠实现各向异性模稳定，从而获得一个或两个大额外维度（分别对应ADD和暗维度场景）。通过微扰修正（弦圈和高阶导数效应）将4D K3纤维体积稳定在较小值，而2D P^1基的体积则指数级大。复结构模的稳定可动态形变P^1基，对应Tyurin退化极限，使内禀几何发展出单个大的一维环。ADD情况则作为对称替代极限恢复。势能可支持dS真空或精质跑动，但两种情形均需一定调谐以匹配观测宇宙学常数。论文还给出了具有一致膜配置、tadpole消除和模稳定的显式Calabi-Yau定向折示例，分析了模谱及相关现象学约束（超对称破缺、宇宙学模过产生和第五力界限）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在IIB型大体积场景中，选用K3纤维化于P^1基的Calabi-Yau三折叠，利用弦圈修正和高阶导数效应稳定K3纤维体积，通过复结构模稳定驱动Tyurin退化极限实现P^1基的各向异性形变，统一描述ADD极限和暗维度极限。结合显式定向折模型验证tadpole消除和模稳定性。

Result: 实现了各向异性弦紧化，可自然产生一个（暗维度）或两个（ADD）大额外维度，得到dS真空或精质跑动势能，但需调谐宇宙学常数；给出了显式Calabi-Yau定向折示例并分析了模谱和现象学约束。

Conclusion: 成功在IIB型弦论中构建了各向异性大额外维度的模稳定机制，统一描述了ADD和暗维度场景，为后续弦现象学研究（如超对称破缺、第五力等）提供了具体可操作的框架。

Abstract: We provide a moduli stabilisation mechanism for realising anisotropic string compactifications with one or two large extra dimensions, corresponding to the ADD and Dark Dimension scenarios. This is achieved within the type IIB Large Volume Scenario, where an exponentially large Calabi-Yau volume in string units can naturally generate a parametrically low Kaluza-Klein scale. Anisotropy is realised by considering a Calabi-Yau threefold which is a K3 fibration over a $\mathbb{P}^1$ base. The volume of the 4D K3 fibre is stabilised at relatively small values by perturbative corrections to the effective action, in particular string loops and higher-derivative effects, leaving an exponentially large volume of the 2D $\mathbb{P}^1$ base. We argue that complex structure moduli stabilisation can dynamically deform the $\mathbb{P}^1$ base, corresponding to a Tyurin degeneration limit where the internal geometry effectively develops a single large 1D cycle. Within a unified description, the ADD case is instead recovered as a symmetric alternative limit. The potential can feature either a dS vacuum or a quintessence runaway, although in both cases some degree of tuning is required to match the observed cosmological constant scale. We also present an explicit Calabi-Yau orientifold example with consistent brane setup, tadpole cancellation and moduli stabilisation. We analyse the resulting moduli spectrum and associated phenomenological constraints, including supersymmetry breaking, cosmological moduli overproduction and fifth force bounds.

*Stefan A. Kurlyand*

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了Freund-Rubin背景AdS4×Y7中的欧几里得M2膜瞬子，证明了Y7为弱G2流形时M2膜包裹三维圈的条件等价于近G2结构下的结合性条件；在Sasaki-Einstein情形下识别了一类保持实内禀Killing旋量的BPS M2膜，并将涨落问题简化为横截椭圆复形，利用等变指标公式计算了单圈配分函数；最后应用于S7/Zk和(p,q)模型几何中的具体瞬子实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究AdS4×Y7背景中M2膜瞬子的BPS条件与几何结构的关系，并系统计算其量子涨落和单圈配分函数。

Method: 利用弱G2流形和Sasaki-Einstein流形的几何性质，将BPS条件转化为几何条件；通过横截椭圆复形和等变指标公式分析涨落并计算配分函数。

Result: 阐明了M2膜BPS条件与弱G2结合性的等价关系；在Sasaki-Einstein情形下识别出保持双实Killing旋量的特殊BPS膜；将单圈配分函数用等变指标表示，并成功复现S7/Zk中S3/Zk瞬子的已知结果。

Conclusion: 为AdS/CFT对应中M2膜瞬子的微扰计算提供了系统的几何框架和计算方法。

Abstract: We study Euclidean M2-brane instantons in Freund-Rubin backgrounds $\mathrm{AdS}_{4}\times \mathrm{Y}_7$. For a seven-dimensional weak $G_{2}$ manifold $\mathrm{Y}_7$, we show that the BPS condition for an M2-brane wrapping a three-cycle $Σ\subset \mathrm{Y}_7$ is equivalent to the associativity condition with respect to the nearly parallel $G_{2}$-structure. When $\mathrm{Y}_7$ is Sasaki-Einstein, we identify a special class of BPS M2-branes that preserve both real internal Killing spinors and correspond to invariant three-dimensional submanifolds inheriting a Sasakian structure. We analyse the quadratic fluctuations around BPS M2-brane instantons in these backgrounds. For the special class of M2-branes in Sasaki-Einstein manifolds, the fluctuation problem reduces to transversely elliptic complexes, and the one-loop partition function can be expressed in terms of the corresponding equivariant indices. We then apply the index formula for the one-loop partition function to invariant M2-branes in $S^{7}/\mathbb{Z}_{k}$, recovering the known result for the $S^3/\mathbb{Z}_k$ instantons and discussing more general invariant BPS cycles. As a further application, we consider M2-brane instantons with $S^3$-quotient worldvolumes in the $(p,q)$-model geometry.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入边界管代数（Tube algebra）和对称性约束的测量资源理论，通过完全正定性、纠缠切割局域性、边界模协变性、序列稳定性四条公理刻画物理允许的测量仪器，进而证明最优测量结构由边界管代数的中心决定，构造管POVM。

Conclusion: 建立了融合范畴普适的量子态区分性变分原理，统一并推广了标准保真度和对称性分解方法，为广义对称性多体系统中的量子测量和假设检验提供了严格的操作性框架。

Abstract: A variational principle for quantum-state distinguishability is established in many-body systems with generalized symmetries, including noninvertible cases described by fusion categories. Standard fidelity and symmetry-resolved diagnostics emerge as coarse-grained limits of a more refined operational structure. When symmetry actions terminate at entanglement cuts, distinguishability is governed by boundary tube algebras within a symmetry-constrained measurement resource theory. The physically admissible instruments are characterized by complete positivity, entanglement-cut locality, boundary-module covariance, and sequential stability. The resulting optimal measurement structure is uniquely fixed by the center of the boundary tube algebra, $\mathcal{A}_{\mathrm{phys}} = Z\!\left(\mathrm{Tube}_{\mathcal{C}}(\mathcal{M}_A)\right)$, whose primitive idempotents define tube-sector probabilities that refine fidelity-based and symmetry-resolved descriptions. Abstract: In this article, we present four different $1+1$D quantum models that realize the Yang-Lee (YL) phase transition under a deformation that preserves $PT$ symmetry. Using the state-operator correspondence, we identify the YL critical point, compute the scaling dimensions of the lowest operators in each model, and find perfect agreement with the exact results for the YL criticality in two dimensions. In the quantum clock model, this critical field interacts with a massive bosonic field, and we identify the massless and massive states in the Hamiltonian spectrum. In addition, we numerically compute the two-point function of $φ$ at the Yang-Lee critical point and show that it grows with distance, in agreement with theoretical expectations.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决黑洞信息悖论，即霍金辐射导致信息丢失的问题。传统霍金辐射会持续到黑洞完全蒸发，但该论文提出辐射在 scrambling 时间后因跨普朗克相互作用的非局域效应而提前终止，从而保留信息在宏观残余物中。

Method: 通过弦场论中的平滑算子 $e^{\ell^2\Box}$（$\ell$ 为弦长尺度）修改无质量标量场与动态黑洞背景的相互作用，计算了出射霍金粒子在延迟时间 $u$ 上的时间依赖数期望值 $\langle \hat{N}(u) \rangle$。

Result: 早期时间（$u \ll u_{\text{scr}}$）再现了霍金温度下的标准普朗克谱，但在 scrambling 时间后不久粒子数趋近于零。这表明坍缩壳对跨普朗克模式变得有效不可见，辐射提前关闭。

Conclusion: 霍金辐射在 scrambling 时间终止，而非持续到黑洞完全蒸发，这为黑洞信息悖论提供了一种替代性解决方案，即信息保留在宏观残余物中，避免了信息丢失问题。

Abstract: We demonstrate that, for a large black hole of radius $a$, Hawking radiation terminates around the scrambling time $u_{\text{scr}} \equiv 2a \log(a/\ell)$ due to the nonlocal, exponential suppression of trans-Planckian interactions inherent in string field theory (SFT). Modifying a massless scalar field's interaction with a dynamical black hole background via the smearing operator $e^{\ell^2\Box}$ (where $\ell$ denotes the string length scale), we calculate the time-dependent number expectation value $\langle \hat{N}(u) \rangle$ of outgoing Hawking particles at retarded time $u$. While the standard Planck spectrum at the Hawking temperature is reproduced at early times ($u \ll u_{\text{scr}}$), the particle number approaches zero shortly after the scrambling time. This early shutoff reflects the property that the collapsing shell becomes effectively invisible to trans-Planckian modes, offering an alternative resolution to the black hole information paradox via a macroscopic remnant.

</details>

Result: 真空中普朗克尺度涨落之间存在随距离缓慢衰减的关联（扩展尺度关联）；这种关联能“感知”闭合俘获面即将形成的区域，并通过成核fuzzball结构来破坏半经典时空。
